  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9c7ec5fd-88dc-4868-971f-88af52f7d788'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1276048101?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2015</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1276048101" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer808954200651743700"><br/>No words. Should have sent a poet.<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/YkWDRee' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438400571i/15702742.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>Okay, I lied. I may have a *<i>few</i>* words (I am still <i>me</i> after all,) but in all seriousness...<br/><br/>        <b>I. Loved. This. Magical. Book.    (<i>Literally</i>)</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/bgD3WhJ' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438402861ra/15702881.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>From start to finish, <b>I was never bored</b>, not even for a single paragraph of its considerable <b>400+ page</b> length.<br/><br/><b>Sam of Wilds</b> is a 20 y.o. wizard's apprentice (to Morgan of Shadows,) with more <b>blurty, unfiltered goodness</b> in him than one could possibly imagine. And it was a (slightly blinding) sight to behold.<br/><br/>Sam'</span>
  <span id="freeText808954200651743700" style="display:none"><br>No words. Should have sent a poet.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/YkWDRee" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438400571i/15702742.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Okay, I lied. I may have a *<i>few</i>* words (I am still <i>me</i> after all,) but in all seriousness...<br><br>        <b>I. Loved. This. Magical. Book.    (<i>Literally</i>)</b> <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/bgD3WhJ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438402861ra/15702881.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>From start to finish, <b>I was never bored</b>, not even for a single paragraph of its considerable <b>400+ page</b> length.<br><br><b>Sam of Wilds</b> is a 20 y.o. wizard's apprentice (to Morgan of Shadows,) with more <b>blurty, unfiltered goodness</b> in him than one could possibly imagine. And it was a (slightly blinding) sight to behold.<br><br>Sam's best friend is <b>Gary</b>, a hornless gay unicorn. And folks, he is a <b>fierce, snarky BITCH</b>, so watch out or someone's going to lose a testicle.<br><br>Gary's also a wee bit vain. Just a touch.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/fknenG7" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438402323i/15702847.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sam's other best friend is <b>Tiggy</b>, a nine-foot-tall half-giant, who may not be the brightest marble in the bag, but he protects Sam and Gary with a fury best not tested. It's a good way to be wearing your insides on your outsides. And quickly.<br><br>Then we have Sam's <i>would-be love interest</i>, 25 y.o. <b>Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart</b>, who makes everyone in the kingdom swoon.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/kNwCbrr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438401537i/15702806._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But Sam most of all, who <i>very secretly</i> attends meetings of the <b>Ryan Foxheart Fan Club</b>. That plot point was crazy funny.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The one and only time that I went...”<br><br>“Of the four times that I've been...”<br><br>“On my eighth time there...”<br><br>“Of the twenty-six times that I've attended...”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Hilarious.<br><br>But there's the small matter of <b>Ryan's engagement to Prince Justin</b> (who you <b>will</b> immediately want to junk punch at first sight) standing in the way of our two heroes' happiness.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/mnk6OOo" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438403515ra/15702909.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The interactions between Sam and Ryan are freaking priceless. Price. Less.<br><br>They both seem to be vying for the coveted title of <b>Most Clueless Where Attractions Are Concerned</b>. Yes, I capitalized it, because it's a thing. ;- ) (Sam does that a lot in the book as well, which I found cute and endearing.)<blockquote>
  <b><i>“You capitalized that, didn’t you,”</i> Morgan sighed. <br><i>“I did,”</i> I said. <i>“That’s how you know it’s epic.”</i> <br>Gary’s rage glitter subsided. <i>“The most epic there could be.”</i></b>
</blockquote>Sam doesn't believe that Ryan even knows he exists (he's ooooh so wrong) and, without fail, <b>squeaks and runs away whenever he sees Ryan</b>, which had been happening for 5 years running.<br><br>But when <b>a dragon kidnaps Prince Justin</b> (yay and good riddance to bad rubbish, I say), the King requests that Sam accompany Ryan on a <b>quest to rescue Prince Justin</b>.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Yaaaay." *slow-clap*</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/tDYd54K" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438406525ra/15703067.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And thus Sam's <b>Plan to Avoid Ryan at All Costs</b> comes to a swift and abrupt end. Yes, again capitalized, because it's <i>a thing</i>.<br><br>God, their back and forth was a true thing of beauty, as spending week after week together begins to solidify the <b>previously-uncharted longing</b> in their hearts.<br><br>But, sadly, <b>there's still Prince Justin</b>, who they've been sent to rescue.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Dear Dragon, I've heard Justin is quite delicious. Bon appetite! I'll supply dessert. *Kisses*"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <a href="http://imgur.com/WskVPe9" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438406834ra/15703094.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, yeah, while the book has <b>an unending supply of longing and want</b>, neither Sam nor Ryan are the home-wrecking or cheating type and they avoid revealing their true feelings at all costs.<br><br>I'm sure, that like myself, some readers will comment as to <b>a lack of relationship building</b>; however, as the story was written, I didn't see how that could have really come about -- <b>without them cheating.</b><br><br>So I understood and just went with the happy, blurty, fairly-uncomfortable flow between Sam and Ryan, enjoying the ride and allowing events to play out.<br><br>And, Christ, how Sam was tested during that journey.<blockquote>
  <b>Now was Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart climbing slowly out of the river, water cascading down his body, dripping over miles and miles of muscle. He wore nothing but a thin, white undergarment that stuck and clung to his groin and thighs. He reached down, the muscles in his back flexing as he scooped up water in his hands and brought it up and over his head. His nipples were pebbled. His chest was covered in a smattering of wet hair. He was lines and corded muscle, definition and carved from stone. If I had let my eyes linger, I would have sworn I could see the outline of his cock through the wet fabric. My skin felt tight and flushed and I <i>wanted</i>. There was green and gold, and it was so fucking bright that I almost had to shut my eyes from the weight of it. <br><br><i>“I swear he’s doing this on purpose,”</i> Gary whispered hotly. <br><br><i>“I swear I want to do him on purpose,”</i> I breathed. <br><br>Gary choked and I didn’t care. <br><br>I would never have him. I knew this. It wasn’t meant to be. <br><br>But that didn’t mean I couldn’t be creepy and have this one <i>fucking moment</i> where I could pretend and wish and hope and dream and yes, now I had an erection and it was fucking <i>awful</i>.</b>
</blockquote><b>HAWT!</b><br><br>Okay, that's all for possible spoilers, folks. I refuse to be <i>"that bitch"</i>, so no more plot points, but I will lastly divulge that:<blockquote>1.) <b>Sam and Ryan do (as expected) get their happily ever after.</b> <br><br>        -- and --<br><br>2.) The <b>sexy scenes</b>, once they finally, finally <i>FINALLY</i> get together, are <i>almost</i> <b>worth the wait and very worthy of the rest of this very good book</b>. <br><br>** I only say '<i>almost</i>' because I tend to be an impatient bitch, but if they had cheated, it would've ruined the entire experience for me, so I'm truly thankful that they didn't.</blockquote><a href="http://imgur.com/fVs6HaL" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438401256i/15702784._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In this book, <b>the banter is non-stop</b>, which I personally loved. For me, that was a good thing, keeping me fully-engaged.<br><br>But <b>be warned</b>, much the same as some readers felt that TJ's <b>"Tell Me It's Real"</b> was way <b>over-the-top</b>, there's <b>much the same feel</b> in this book.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/xESdeRa" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438401101i/15702777._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So if I had to make a guess, if you loved <b>Paul and Sandy's banter</b> in "Tell Me It's Real," then I *think* you will love this one, too. <br><br>However, if you hated that type of humor, this book has *way* more of it than TMIR ever dared dream, so keep that in mind when deciding to read.<br><br>But honestly? <b>I wouldn't have changed a thing</b> and can't wait to read the next book, which there had better be <b>or somebody's gonna die in a Shit Storm of Glittery Unicorn Rage</b>.<br><br>Yes, I <i>capitalized it</i>, because it's an honest-to-God thing, people! ;- )<br><br>It's been a while since a book this long has kept my enrapt attention, so <b>a full 5 motherfucking *Dashing-and-Immaculate* stars</b> for this ridiculously fun, epic tale.<br><br>---------------------------------<br><br>My ARC copy of the book was provided by the publisher in exchange for a fair, unbiased review.<br><br>---------------------------------<br><br><b>** UPDATE 10/2015:</b> <br><br>TJ has a *FREE* 50'ish page Tina DeSilva follow-up story for The Lightning Struck Heart on his blog! *tingles*<br><br><b>Tales From Verania: The Tragic Life of Lady Tina DeSilva</b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tjklunebooks.blogspot.com/2015/09/tales-from-verania-tragic-life-of-lady.html">http://tjklunebooks.blogspot.com/2015...</a><br><br>---------------------------------</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1331370034" />
    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1331370034?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=losing-the-v-card">losing-the-v-card</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=read-to-review-arc">read-to-review-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=little-to-no-sex-content">little-to-no-sex-content</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=magic">magic</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1331370034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer416091313348626538"><b>*Kindle Freebie 3/22/18!!*</b><br/><br/><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br/><br/>Soooooo much to say about this one! First of all, I'm a MEGA <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune' title='T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>T.J. Klune</a> fan. I love his particular brand of humor and I think that he is an extremely talented writer. I preface with that because all of you should know that my rating and review is coming from someone who is a self-proclaimed T.J. fangirl.<br/><br/><b>So what do you need to know about this one? What is the deal with this story? I'll break it down for all of you.</b> <br/><br/><u>The characters.</u><br/><br/>If you have read a T.J. book r</span>
  <span id="freeText416091313348626538" style="display:none"><b>*Kindle Freebie 3/22/18!!*</b><br /><br /><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br /><br />Soooooo much to say about this one! First of all, I'm a MEGA <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> fan. I love his particular brand of humor and I think that he is an extremely talented writer. I preface with that because all of you should know that my rating and review is coming from someone who is a self-proclaimed T.J. fangirl.<br /><br /><b>So what do you need to know about this one? What is the deal with this story? I'll break it down for all of you.</b> <br /><br /><u>The characters.</u><br /><br />If you have read a T.J. book recently, you are already well acquainted with the characters in this book. No, these are not people who we've seen before, but they are strikingly similar to some of T.J.'s greatest from his previous books. In the same way that Bear, Ty, and Paul had no filter and sort of just blurted out ridiculous things, so does Sam, the main character here. He is the same funny, everyone loves him but sort of wants to kill him, person as we've seen before in many of T.J.'s books. That isn't a bad thing, but it rings very familiar. <br /><br />I really liked Sam, even though he was willfully oblivious to the point of painful. It was also a little annoying how everyone, and I mean EVERYONE, loved him, but I still found him to be a great protagonist. However, my favorite characters were Tiggy (I SMASH!! You'll see...) and Gary. I just LOVED the idea of a horn-less unicorn who was into some weird, freaky-deaky sex stuff. Gary, you bad boy you. He just cracked me up! I also loved Ryan, (aka Knight Delicious Face). I toootally got the appeal, and I also wanted to squish his sexy face and bone him. <br /><br /><u>The humor.</u><br /><br />Now, this is where my warning comes into play: <b>THIS BOOK IS FOR T.J. KLUNE FANS ONLY. The humor is non-stop, every page is just ON, and if you found previous T.J. Klune books to be over-the-top, you will not like this one.</b> This book is even more over-the-top, with each page sort of getting more and more ridiculous. The banter is constant. I looooved the back and forth between the characters, I loved the nicknames, I loved the humor, but even I, a HUGE T.J. Fan, could see how it could becomes tiresome. <b>In my opinion, it was incredibly enjoyable to read a book that was so light and fun.</b> <br /><br /><u>The world-building.</u><br /><br />I'd call this <b>fantasy ultra-light</b>. Though this is set in a fantasy world with knights, wizards, and magical creatures, there are a ton of pop-culture references (from our world), and the world-building is shaky at best. I think the fantasy realm is meant as another vehicle for T.J.'s imagination, and this book is not meant as a heavy-duty fantasy novel. For example, the King jokes around with Sam like he is Sam's bestie and not a ruler of the kingdom. There is NO formality in the castle, and everyone gets in on the puns, joking, and sexual innuendoes. <br /><br /><u>The plot.</u><br /><br />Now this is where I found this book to be a little... sticky. This book is super long, clocking in at 400+ pages, and I think it could have been cut down a lot. The beginning, especially, is really repetitive. While there is a story arc, the book is mostly just one zany happening after the other. I also wish the editor had been a bit more careful because I found numerous grammatical mistakes, which always irks me. <br /><br /><u>The romance.</u><br /><br />The romance element of this book grew on me more and more. For almost the entire book, Ryan is engaged to someone else. That made the relationship-building element a little difficult for me to get on board with. However, over time, I grew to be totally team HaveHeart and a big Foxy Lady (you'll see...), and I was SOOO ready for these two guys to just get their act together! I also understood the attraction between the two men a little more as the book went on. <br /><br /><u>Sex content.</u><br /><br /><b>Ladies and gentlemen, there is almost no sex in this book.</b> Be prepared. Just one tiny scene with some nookie, but if you are looking for some detailed action, look elsewhere. <br /><br /><u>Moral of the story.</u><br /><br /><b>If you love T.J. and you can't get enough of his particular brand of humor, you will simply adore this one. It is lighthearted but heartfelt, and though I think it could have used some tweaking, it was a classically funny T.J. read with a beautiful HEA. </b><br /><br />*Copy provided by the publisher in exchange for an honest review*</span>
  <a data-text-id="416091313348626538" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1340273402" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11404245386640566544">It was time for yet another re-read. This book always manages to make me smile and feel better. Thanks TJ ;) 2/2020<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495558018i/22830571.jpg' alt='FOTO BEWERKEN - makkelijk online je foto's bewerken of aanpassen: ' width='235' height='78' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am not even gonna try and explain the whole storyline of this book. It is way too complicated and ridiculous to explain. What I will tell you, is that everybody should read this book !! I can honestly say that this book will probably be my favorite read of 2016...and the year has just begun. That's how awesome this book is.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387551940ra/7618605.gif' alt='Afbeeldingsresultaat voor so awesome + gif' width='317' height='161' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you want to step into a world of magic and creatures an</span>
  <span id="freeText11404245386640566544" style="display:none">It was time for yet another re-read. This book always manages to make me smile and feel better. Thanks TJ ;) 2/2020<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495558018i/22830571.jpg" alt="FOTO BEWERKEN - makkelijk online je foto's bewerken of aanpassen: " width="235" height="78" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am not even gonna try and explain the whole storyline of this book. It is way too complicated and ridiculous to explain. What I will tell you, is that everybody should read this book !! I can honestly say that this book will probably be my favorite read of 2016...and the year has just begun. That's how awesome this book is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387551940ra/7618605.gif" alt="Afbeeldingsresultaat voor so awesome + gif" width="317" height="161" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you want to step into a world of magic and creatures and romance, all while laughing your ass off at every page, then you should start reading this one ..right now !!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495558018ra/22830573.gif" width="340" height="191" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is about Sam of Wilds a 20-year-old wizard apprentice and his two best friends...... Gary, a snarky and sassy gay hornless unicorn and Tiggy a sweet and very protective half-giant, who loves to smash things.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495558018i/22830574.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then there is also the man Sam has been crushing on since he was 15 years old (and with crushing I mean jerking off while fantasizing about him). The dashing and immaculate Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart.<br><br><em>
  <strong>“Look. This has been… fun.” Lie. This had been nerve-racking and I needed to go masturbate. “But I have to go. I’ve got stuff to do before I head out again.” Masturbate. “Wizard stuff. Like… secret wizard stuff.” Masturbate.</strong>
</em><br><br>Too bad Ryan is about to be married to the prince of Varnia, prince Justin...the same prince, Sam will serve in the future, when he becomes king.<br><br>When Justin gets kidnapped by a dragon, it's up to Sam, Gary, Tiggy, and Ryan, to go and rescue the man. Which is the start of one of the funniest "adventures" I have ever read about.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495558018ra/22830575.gif" alt="Afbeeldingsresultaat voor i almost peed my pants + gif" width="362" height="212" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like I said...I can't go into the plot much further, because really....it's too much to explain and I probably wouldn't make much sense. It was sooooo good and it made me soooo freaking happy :) I think TJ Klune himself is magical .....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495558018ra/22830576.gif" alt="Afbeeldingsresultaat voor you are magical + gif" width="224" height="224" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can't wait for the other books in this series !!!!<br><br>If I could give this one 10 stars I would, but I will just give it the 5 well-deserved ones ;) <br><br>I haven't laughed this hard in a long time :)))<br><br><blockquote>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1340170439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2218176663275169572"><b>Re-read October 2020</b><br/>This is the one book I can read over and over again and never get enough of.<br/><br/>----------------------------------<br/><b>BEST BOOK EVER!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443006110ra/16305914.gif' width='380' height='260' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I freaking LOVED this book. <br/><br/>This book is hilarious. But it was also beautiful, sweet, and it broke my heart in the best way possible(because there is so much pining, it was awesome).<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“It’s you,” I said, not able to look away. “It’s how I feel when I’m with you. How I think I’ve always felt. You’re my lightning-struck heart. Ever since I’ve known you,</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText2218176663275169572" style="display:none"><b>Re-read October 2020</b><br>This is the one book I can read over and over again and never get enough of.<br><br>----------------------------------<br><b>BEST BOOK EVER!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443006110ra/16305914.gif" width="380" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I freaking LOVED this book. <br><br>This book is hilarious. But it was also beautiful, sweet, and it broke my heart in the best way possible(because there is so much pining, it was awesome).<br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s you,” I said, not able to look away. “It’s how I feel when I’m with you. How I think I’ve always felt. You’re my lightning-struck heart. Ever since I’ve known you, you’ve struck my heart, and now I have to let you go because you’re not mine to keep. I need someone that I can be strong for. But I need someone who can also be strong for me.”</i>
</b><br><br>I cannot express my love for Sam enough. Sam, a 20 year old wizard apprentice. The most powerful there is actually. Sam, who doesn’t know how to shut up, ever. And his pining for Ryan was just EPIC.<br><br><b>
  <i>Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart was climbing slowly out of the river, water cascading down his body, dripping over miles and miles of muscle.<br>“I swear he’s doing this on purpose,” Gary whispered hotly.<br>“I swear I want to do him on purpose,” I breathed.<br>“You okay, Sam? ” Ryan asked, and his voice was husky.<br>So I blurted out, “I’ve got wood.” Gary turned his head slowly to gape at me. <br>“Oh dear gods,” I muttered. Then louder, “Wood. I brought the wood. I’ve got so much wood. Wood. Fuck. Firewood. I’ve got firewood. For the fire. Because it’s going to get nipples out tonight. Cold. It’s going to get cold out tonight. Sweet molasses.”</i>
</b><br><br>And Ryan, I loved Ryan. He was awesome.<br><br><b>
  <i>I’ve heard of you… people.”<br>Oh gods. Mama cocked her head at him. To most, it wouldn’t have seemed like anything. But for those that knew her, Mama was coiling to strike.<br>“What do you mean by you people?” she asked.<br>I had to stop the bloodshed before it could start. “He means—”<br>“Pimps,” Ryan said. “Is that what you’re called? Pimps? Brothel owner? Whoremaster? Queen of the Fuck Palace?”</i>
</b><br><br>And how can I express my love for all the other amazing characters..<br><br>Gary, the gay hornless unicorn. <br><br><b>
  <i>“When were you tied up? ”I asked again.<br> “It was that centaur we met last year. In the elf realm.”<br>“You said you were just friends!”<br>“We were. We were just the kind of friends that tied each other up and pushed our penises together.”</i>
</b><br><br>Tiggy, the half giant.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You want mouth full of knight,” Tiggy said. “Knight take your flower and eat it.”</i>
</b><br><br>Kevin, the dragon.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Why are we even out here!”<br>“Bonding,” Kevin said. “ You said that we needed bonding.” Then he leered at me, his lip curling, tongue snaking out between his fangs. “Or perhaps you meant bondage? Is that what you meant, pretty? You need me to tie you up and choke you on my dick? Make you scream as I twist your little nipples? Make you—”<br>“That’s not what I meant at all.”</i>
</b><br><br>The king.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Okay, so, how would you feel if you looked like you had boobs?” <br>“Is that a hypothetical question? ” the king said.<br>“Hypothetically… no. More like that’s what I painted somehow and will now be a part of the finished product because I don’ t know how to fix it. Nor do I know if I want to.”<br>“Am I busty?”<br>“Very. You also have three of them.”<br>“Good. Proceed.”</i>
</b><br><br>I have so much love for them all.<br><br>Yes, the romance mostly consists of pining for each other without any sexy times (there are sexy times, don't worry!). It took Ryan a while to get his head out of his ass. Especially since Sam had no idea how Ryan was feeling.<br><br>Until the truth corn of course. No way around it after that.<br><br><b>
  <i>”When you do anything, I get hard, really. Even your ridiculous sex puns. You remember when you wrapped those Dark wizards in stone at the restaurant?”<br>“Yeah,” I managed to say.<br>“I wanted to tell you that you gave me an e-rock-tion.” Ryan bent over and banged his forehead against the table. “Why, why, why did I say that out loud? Please. Someone. Anyone. Kill me.”</i>
</b><br><br>It takes a long time for these two to get together, but it was worth the wait. I sighed, I swooned, and to steal Gary’s words, I got a heart boner.<br><br>This book had everything I ever wanted in a book. A fairy tale with a magical hero who is socially awkward yet also very awesome in his ramblings, cool sidekicks, extremely funny situations and a lovely HEA.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471349596ra/20033499.gif" width="380" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1321532660" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1321532660" />
    <a title="wesley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36179338-wesley"><img alt="wesley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446832327p2/36179338.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1321532660?book_show_action=true">Jun 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="wesley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="wesley" href="/user/show/36179338-wesley">wesley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=friendship">friendship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=wizards">wizards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=mm-funny">mm-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=not-your-easy-love">not-your-easy-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=sweet-as-sugar">sweet-as-sugar</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=root-for-the-underdog">root-for-the-underdog</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1321532660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6179479861262650233"><p>First of all, I just want to let it be known that this book deserves to have a sequel, no matter how obvious it was that it certainly will. But just so there’s no sliver of doubt and I can have peace of mind, I’ll say it again: <u>The Lightning-Struck Heart must have a sequel</u>. No, scratch that. <u>The Lightning-Struck Heart cannot <i>not</i> have <i>sequelssss</i></u>. You hear me T.J. Klune? Huh? Huh?! (I’m not really good at taunting authors.)</p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439382598ra/15828469.gif' alt='Give it to me' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><p>Now that I’ve finally let it out, onto the review!</p><p>If you are a hardcore fan</p></span>
  <span id="freeText6179479861262650233" style="display:none"><p>First of all, I just want to let it be known that this book deserves to have a sequel, no matter how obvious it was that it certainly will. But just so there’s no sliver of doubt and I can have peace of mind, I’ll say it again: <u>The Lightning-Struck Heart must have a sequel</u>. No, scratch that. <u>The Lightning-Struck Heart cannot <i>not</i> have <i>sequelssss</i></u>. You hear me T.J. Klune? Huh? Huh?! (I’m not really good at taunting authors.)</p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439382598ra/15828469.gif" alt="Give it to me" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>Now that I’ve finally let it out, onto the review!</p><p>If you are a hardcore fan of fantasy books, magic, wizards, and medieval kingdoms, you may think, <i>“Pffft! Puh-lease! I’ve seen (or read) it all.”</i> But if you haven’t read this book, I can assure you that you haven’t seen it all. And that’s probably my cue to throw the book right on your smug face. Although, I’m not really a fan of violence and that’s kind of cruel to the book, and I only have my iPhone for a reading device so that would be unwise and stupid. But you get the point, yeah?</p><p>To say that this book is epic and awesome would be an understatement. So to give it justice, I’ll follow Sam of Wilds with the whole capitalization thing such that this book officially is <b>The Most Awesome and Epic Fantasy Book of All Time!</b> God, that felt great.</p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439382938ra/15828485.gif" alt="epic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>In all honesty though, I’ve never had the pleasure of reading a book of this caliber. It felt like being high all the time. Okay, not a good metaphor but still! Everything was just amped up – like every time your favorite song comes on the radio and you can’t help turning the volume to max. </p><p>And I dare ask: How does T.J. do that? This was beyond any normal level of hilarious and witty. I was worried I’d have bad gas from the nonstop laughing. I was practically crying and wheezing. It was like this book was written especially for my generation. Make no mistake, the book was set during the medieval times but it was more like being in an alternate universe where the medieval people are updated with everything happening on social media and the contemporary gibberish of our era.</p><p>
  <i>“You mad, bro?”</i>
</p><p>
  <i>“Love you, boo!”</i>
</p><p>
  <i>“Dat. Ass.”</i>
</p><p>
  <i>“Baby. Look at me. Hey. Baby. Listen.”</i>
</p><p>
  <i>“Ooooh, girl!”</i>
</p><p>
  <i>“Don’t need no mens.”</i>
</p><p>And the sarcasm? The banter? The cursing and the dirty talk? The sex puns? Never forget the sex puns.</p><p>Genius and uncensored! Exasperatingly funny, but genius nonetheless. I think this broke all literary conventions. It was practicing poetic license at its finest.</p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439383475ra/15828568.gif" alt="genius" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>And I see where your mind is going. I know you’re thinking, <i>“If the 171K of words is mostly this kind of shit, where’s the story? Is there any substance at all?”</i> Yeah, I read your mind, buddy. I’m also a wizard. No, I’m not. But if you’re worried there’s no concrete plot, I’m quoting Sam when he reflected on the many (and I say that exaggeratedly) twists he went through:</p><blockquote>
  <b>That night, I lay on my back on the roof of the keep, watching the stars above, wondering just how in the hell my life had gotten to this point.<br><br>Then I realized it was mostly my fault, and that made me sort of depressed and happy all at the same time.<br><br>I told myself that it was because I was extraordinarily complex.</b>
</blockquote><p>I’m stopping there because you don’t want to know the rest of what he said (<u>spoiler</u>: he contradicted the whole thing). But I do agree (before he contradicted himself). Despite the shenanigans and the madfuckery that this book contain, the story was extraordinarily complex. It was unpredictable and unconventional. Each chapter practically a subplot of epic proportions. And the characters? Dynamic and non-stereotypical. All of them, even the secondary characters, were unique and bursting with vibrant personality. Reading their banter was endearing. Well, in the case of Sam and Ryan – frustratingly arousing and coated with deep sexual tension. I never expected to be affected by it so much, I had the case of blue balls for 3 days. Yes, imagine! Or don’t imagine. But foreplay with just words? Talk about enlightening!</p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439384153ra/15828636.gif" alt="boner" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>Okay, I got a little sidetracked there. But yeah, if you’re worried about the storyline, don’t. I assure you, this has the right mix of humor and a great plot going on. You have to hand it to Sam though. I was mostly drawn to him. Yeah, he was badass and all kinds of awesome but that’s not the reason you will love him. Even though he will probably be the greatest wizard of all time, I was warmed by his vulnerability. He is an underdog through and through and I can't help but empathize with him. He is the epitome of martyrdom and the face of unrequited love. He is a walking irony – powerful and helpless at the same time. He is the heart of this story because it’s his very humanity for which you will feel that deep, resounding connection.</p><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439384153i/15828637._SY540_.png" alt="sam of wilds" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>We’ve all been down that road at one point in our life. The endless pining and the insecurities? Been there, done that.</p><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“There’s someone out there for you. Someone who will love your hair and your words and your eyes and the way you scrunch up your nose when you’re thinking hard on something. He will love you for all of the things that you are and all of the things you aren’t. He’ll love you beyond all reason and will be convinced that you hung the sun and the moon. He will see the stars and wish for only you. Someone will love every single part of who you are, and my gods, I can’t wait for the day to meet him to tell him thank you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><p>As much as this book made me laugh, I can’t count the number of times I also cried because don’t we all deserve that love? I realized we were (or are or will be) Sam of Wilds at some point in our also badass lives. We also wish the same things he did. We also give it everything we’ve got. Because of this, Sam will probably be one of my most favorite protagonists of all time.</p><p>T.J. Klune, you are my new hero! Thank you for sharing your literary gift to the world. If there are Sam Girls, then I can unabashedly say that I am most definitely a T.J. Girl from here on. Secret fan meetings? I'm so down with that!</p> <br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="6179479861262650233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2197417852" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2197417852" />
    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2197417852?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/28177280-the-lightning-struck-heart">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2197417852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7622639051537952782"><b>*Kindle Freebie 3/22/18!!*</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>My original review from 2015 of the book can be found <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1331370034' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a>.</b><br/><br/><u>Previous rating:</u> 3.5 stars<br/><u>Audiobook re-read rating:</u> 3.5 stars for the story, 5+++ stars for the narration = <b>4.5 stars</b> overall<br/><br/>*I'm going to focus the majority of this review on the audio portion. If you want to read a more detailed review on the story then check out my previous review of the ebook.* <br/><br/>Now, I've said this before and I'll say it again- I'm a HUUUUUUGE <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune' title='T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>T.J. Klune</a> fan. HUGE. I've read nearly everythin</span>
  <span id="freeText7622639051537952782" style="display:none"><b>*Kindle Freebie 3/22/18!!*</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>My original review from 2015 of the book can be found <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1331370034" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.</b><br><br><u>Previous rating:</u> 3.5 stars<br><u>Audiobook re-read rating:</u> 3.5 stars for the story, 5+++ stars for the narration = <b>4.5 stars</b> overall<br><br>*I'm going to focus the majority of this review on the audio portion. If you want to read a more detailed review on the story then check out my previous review of the ebook.* <br><br>Now, I've said this before and I'll say it again- I'm a HUUUUUUGE <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> fan. HUGE. I've read nearly everything he has written (I might have missed one book), and I've never given him less than 3.5 stars. He is one of my favorite authors of all time, but this series... yeah, it didn't quite work for me the first time around. <br><br>Don't get me wrong, I <i>liked it</i>, but I found the characters too similar to those from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17194490.Tell_Me_It_s_Real__At_First_Sight___1_" title="Tell Me It's Real (At First Sight, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Tell Me It's Real</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12156759.Bear__Otter__and_the_Kid__Bear__Otter__and_the_Kid___1_" title="Bear, Otter, and the Kid (Bear, Otter, and the Kid, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Bear, Otter, and the Kid</a>, and the plot to be too long with too much meandering. Of course, I adored the humor (as all die-hard TJ fans would), but I felt exasperated by the end by how long it took the MCs to get together. <br><br>I was ready to put this whole series aside with a shrug, but all of my friends have NOT STOPPED TALKING about the audiobook narration of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24468673.The_Lightning_Struck_Heart__Tales_From_Verania___1_" title="The Lightning-Struck Heart (Tales From Verania, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning-Struck Heart</a>. <br><br>When the audiobook first came out, I was not familiar with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6971140.Michael_Lesley" title="Michael Lesley" rel="nofollow noopener">Michael Lesley</a> so I wasn't willing to take the chance. I hate giving bad ratings to authors that I personally like, so I didn't want to hate the narration and give the book less than 3-stars. However, I decided to take a chance with the audiobook of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17194490.Tell_Me_It_s_Real__At_First_Sight___1_" title="Tell Me It's Real (At First Sight, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Tell Me It's Real</a> (also by Michael Lesley), which is a comfort-read of mine, and see how it went. And it was <i>awesome</i>. So, I figured, what the hell. <br><br><b>I've listened to a LOT of audiobooks (over 250), and I can safely say that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6971140.Michael_Lesley" title="Michael Lesley" rel="nofollow noopener">Michael Lesley</a>'s narration of this book is among the best I've listened to.</b> He was just outstanding, like he OWNED this book, and I am truly stunned as to the quality of the work. Michael mastered no less than 20 separate and unique voices (there are a LOT of side characters!), and put his ALL into the narration. <br><br>It also helps that Michael has just the right cadence, the right delivery, and the right <i>vibe</i> for this story. He sounds young enough to pull off the younger characters but can pitch his voice just so for the older ones. He can do sexy voices, creepy voices, and funny voices. His voice for Tiggy was <i>GOLD</i> (&lt;---my favorite of any of the voices in the book)! <br><br>When I met Michael Lesley in person, he told me that he likes to do accents. I was a little dubious, because a bad accent can be... <i>sad</i>... but his accents were so perfectly done. Sure, it helps that this book is a fantasy so the people don't actually have to be from anywhere in particular, but he made those accents feel natural. <br><br><b>TJ Klune hit the jackpot with him, and he should be thanking his lucky stars that such a perfect-fitting narrator came his way. </b><br><br>My final rating is a full star higher because I really enjoyed the book in audio and Michael Lesley deserves heaps of praise for his work. Still, narration aside, the book is funny, charming, and romantic, even if it won't rank up there in my favorites from TJ. I'm hoping <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30370036.A_Destiny_of_Dragons__Tales_From_Verania___2_" title="A Destiny of Dragons (Tales From Verania, #2) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">A Destiny of Dragons</a> wins me over even more. <br><br>*Copy provided by Dreamspinner Press in exchange for an honest review*</span>
  <a data-text-id="7622639051537952782" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1339789833" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1339789833" />
    <a title="Meags" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8542123-meags"><img alt="Meags" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524277146p2/8542123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1339789833?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Meags" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Meags" href="/user/show/8542123-meags">Meags</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25922661-the-lightning-struck-heart">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=mm-faves">mm-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=fave-characters">fave-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=chuckles-galore">chuckles-galore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=best-of-the-fricken-best">best-of-the-fricken-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=panties-just-went-poof">panties-just-went-poof</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1339789833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6767979575065433668"><b>5 Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24468673.The_Lightning_Struck_Heart__Tales_From_Verania___1_' title='The Lightning-Struck Heart (Tales From Verania, #1) by T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Lightning-Struck Heart</a> is a grand fantasy-adventure, featuring an adorably hilarious wizard's apprentice, his epically awesome parents, his best-friends in the form of a fabulous and fierce gay unicorn and a sweet half-giant, a kind-hearted King and his petulant (but redeemable son), two wizened older wizards, a sex-crazed vegetarian dragon, and a dashing and immaculate young knight. You couldn’t ask for more. <br/><br/>It’s TJ Klune so the writing is obviously of the highest standards. In my e</span>
  <span id="freeText6767979575065433668" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars</b><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24468673.The_Lightning_Struck_Heart__Tales_From_Verania___1_" title="The Lightning-Struck Heart (Tales From Verania, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning-Struck Heart</a> is a grand fantasy-adventure, featuring an adorably hilarious wizard's apprentice, his epically awesome parents, his best-friends in the form of a fabulous and fierce gay unicorn and a sweet half-giant, a kind-hearted King and his petulant (but redeemable son), two wizened older wizards, a sex-crazed vegetarian dragon, and a dashing and immaculate young knight. You couldn’t ask for more. <br /><br />It’s TJ Klune so the writing is obviously of the highest standards. In my eyes, this dude can do no wrong. His stories speak to me, with their perfect blend of heart and humour, and choc-full of the most outrageously fantastic cast of characters the literary world has ever seen.<br /><br />The fantasy elements were also stunning, showcasing a rich and detailed fantasy land, full of mythical creatures and magical beings that effortlessly captured my heart, yet also provided a laugh-a-minute with their ridiculous antics and sassy banter. <br /><br />I laughed hard, to the point of tears on several occasions. I certainly highlighted more than in any book I’ve ever read (112 highlights at last count), re-reading passages over and over again just to absorb the hilarity and genius as much as humanly possible. It was comedy brilliance, pure and simple. <br /><br />But don’t be fooled, as laugh-out-loud funny as this story is, there are also some great feels. The romance between wizard's apprentice Sam Haversford and Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart is the slowest of slow burns, with lots of not-so-subtle flirting and not-so-secret longing. There is frustration and heartache—on my behalf as well as theirs—but in true fairy-tale fashion, there is also the most magical and epic of happily ever after in store for these two oblivious idiots.<br /> <br />I feel like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24468673.The_Lightning_Struck_Heart__Tales_From_Verania___1_" title="The Lightning-Struck Heart (Tales From Verania, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning-Struck Heart</a> was personally tailored to meet my every bookish want and need. Seriously, I have not a single complaint or wish for change in any way, shape or form. To me this was the perfect book, and I have no doubt it will remain a favourite for the rest of my days.<br /><br />*************************************<br /><br /><b>Re-read: July, 2020 (Audio Edition)</b><br /><br />In this audiobook, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24468673.The_Lightning_Struck_Heart__Tales_From_Verania___1_" title="The Lightning-Struck Heart (Tales From Verania, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning-Struck Heart</a> is an already 5 star read made even more magnificent with Michael Lesley’s sensational vocal performance. <br /><br />There aren’t enough superlatives in the dictionary for me to lay adequate praise on Lesley’s narration.<br /><br />It’s comic perfection. <br /><br />It’s pure genius.<br /><br />It’s 100% my favourite audiobook of all time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6767979575065433668" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1166546697" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1166546697" />
    <a title="BWT (Belen)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31775691-bwt-belen"><img alt="BWT (Belen)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1430435406p2/31775691.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1166546697?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="BWT (Belen)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="BWT (Belen)" href="/user/show/31775691-bwt-belen">BWT (Belen)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25922661-the-lightning-struck-heart">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Humor/Feelz lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=mm-fiction">mm-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=gay-book-reviews">gay-book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=mm-favorites">mm-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31775691-bwt-belen?shelf=5-stars-for-real">5-stars-for-real</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1166546697" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11365560949795999601">There aren't enough stars for this...<br/><br/><b><i>The Lightning-Struck Heart</i> or, as it was originally titled, <i>Unicorn Star Fucker</i>, is a fantastic story of love, friendship, longing, loss, and hope.</b><br/><br/><i>Is this funny?</i> Yes. Yes, it is. <b>It's fucking hilarious.</b> Straight up - I was obnoxiously laughing so hard and so loud for so long that I actually began to feel sorry for the people around me. Sorry they were being subjected to my overt hilarity and sorry they were not reading this magnificent and wondrous book so th</span>
  <span id="freeText11365560949795999601" style="display:none">There aren't enough stars for this...<br><br><b><i>The Lightning-Struck Heart</i> or, as it was originally titled, <i>Unicorn Star Fucker</i>, is a fantastic story of love, friendship, longing, loss, and hope.</b><br><br><i>Is this funny?</i> Yes. Yes, it is. <b>It's fucking hilarious.</b> Straight up - I was obnoxiously laughing so hard and so loud for so long that I actually began to feel sorry for the people around me. Sorry they were being subjected to my overt hilarity and sorry they were not reading this magnificent and wondrous book so they too could laugh uproariously.<br><br><i>Does this book make your heart ache?</i> In part. Yes, it will, a little. What can be more sad than wanting someone so desperately, but knowing you can't have him?<br><br><i>"...I’m sorry I made an oath. I did it because I thought it was the right thing to do. And I’m sorry that I can’t break it. But you have to believe me that it’s always been you. I promise. I promise." His voice cracked and my hands shook. "I promise, because when I look upon these stars, there is nothing I wish for more than you."</i><br><br><i>Is this just an OTT Fairy-tale on crack?</i> No. No, it's not. Or, well, it's not <i>only</i> that. There are so many nuances to this. It has humor, heartache, and, most importantly, lessons to be learned about life, love and sometimes letting the things you love go even at the expense of your own heart and soul.<br><br>And, oh, the characters!<br><br>Wizard Apprentice Sam Haversford aka "Sam of Wilds" is maddening, fantastic and wonderful in all his blurty over-the-top goodness. <br><br>Sir Ryan Foxheart, is dashing and wonderful and...an asshole. But not an irredeemable asshole. Which is good.<br><br>The sidekick characters are utterly sublime! (Gary, the hornless gay unicorn, Tiggy, the half-giant, Sam's parents, Morgan and Randall the wizards, Kevin the dragon, Mama, Sam's fairy drag mother, the King, Pete, the guard...<i>gods</i> I could go on and on...) They all steal the spotlight every time they appear on page again and again. <br><br><b>I literally loved every single minute of this.</b><br><br>If you are a fan of Monty Python, Mel Brooks, Top Gun, and The Princess Bride - then you will love this book. You will want to have this book's babies.<br><br>If you are a fan of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a>'s, and love his characters Derrick "Bear" McKenna (BOATK), Paul Auster (TMIR), and Sandy Stewart (TMIR) - then you will love this book. You will beg for more (<i>
  <b>by the way, T.J....MORE PLEASE!!!</b>
</i>) <i>Literally.</i><br><br><img width="400" height="345" alt="description" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437533108i/15595787.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Never fear, dear readers! You get an HEA, but it's also left open for more adventures. And, <i>oh</i>, how I want them. I literally want them so much. <i>Literally.</i><br><br><img width="245" height="200" alt="description" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425255190ra/13868279.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444498076i/16509312.jpg" alt="Belens Audio Book Review" width="150" height="129" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn’t think I could love this story anymore, then I got the audio. <br><br>Michael Lesley takes this funny, makes your heart ache, cracktastic fairy tale and made it infinitely relatable to anyone who loves humor, sarcasm, sassiness, and even sadness.<br><br><b>This is fantastic in all senses of the word. Run, do not walk, to buy this audio!</b><br><br><b>HIGHLY, HIGHLY, HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449954953ra/17361393.gif" alt="coll story bro" width="285" height="281" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>This review has been cross-posted at <a href="http://gaybook.reviews/2015/07/22/the-lightning-struck-heart/" rel="nofollow noopener">Gay Book Reviews</a></i><br><br><i>Audio Review <a href="http://gaybook.reviews/2015/07/22/the-lightning-struck-heart-audio/" rel="nofollow noopener">Gay Book Reviews</a></i><br><br>Read: 07/2015, 08/2015, 09/2015 (2), 12/2015 (2), 02/2016, 08/2016, 11/2016, 01/2017, 03/2017</span>
  <a data-text-id="11365560949795999601" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1173446079?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" href="/user/show/15615404-tara-mindforbooks">Tara♥ {MindforBooks}</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=2015-books">2015-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=dead-tree">dead-tree</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=heroes-i-love">heroes-i-love</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1173446079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10876569375055280739"><b>BR reread for Christmas with Susan, Marte, Doodle, Elsbeth, Heidi and Julie. Perfect holiday reading. Next up the audio! This book is just the best fun and pure comfort reading! <br/><br/>1st read - 20-23 July 2015<br/>2nd read - 18- 28 December 2015</b><br/><br/>_________________________________________<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437734198ra/15623045.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>“You know I captured you and you’re my prisoners, right?"<br/>“Did he?” I asked Gary.<br/>“Well, we are tied up,” Gary said. “And not in the fun way.”<br/>“I don’t want to know when you’ve been tied up in the fun way,” I told him.<br/>He rolled</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10876569375055280739" style="display:none"><b>BR reread for Christmas with Susan, Marte, Doodle, Elsbeth, Heidi and Julie. Perfect holiday reading. Next up the audio! This book is just the best fun and pure comfort reading! <br><br>1st read - 20-23 July 2015<br>2nd read - 18- 28 December 2015</b><br><br>_________________________________________<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437734198ra/15623045.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“You know I captured you and you’re my prisoners, right?"<br>“Did he?” I asked Gary.<br>“Well, we are tied up,” Gary said. “And not in the fun way.”<br>“I don’t want to know when you’ve been tied up in the fun way,” I told him.<br>He rolled his eyes. “Sam, you are such a prude.”<br>“Guys?” Lartin said. “I have a plan? That I need to tell you about? You need to listen.”<br>“I am not a prude,” I said to Gary. “Just because I don’t talk about… you know. Sex stuff. That doesn’t make me a prude.”<br>“Your face just turned red when you stuttered on the word sex,” Gary said. “I almost believed you.”<br>“I didn’t stutter.”<br>“You kind of stuttered,” Lartin said. Because he was an asshole who I was totally going to kick in the balls before the day was up.</b><br><br>Ridiculous, over the top, non stop punning and racing dialogue and I. LOVED. EVERY. SECOND. <br><br>About a quarter of the way through this I got very Monty Python feelings, Monty Python on crack. So you know? Mental. Almost 400 pages of mental. Is it too early for a reread do we think?<br><br>So Monty Python. Specifically The Holy Grail, hence the giffage. I couldn't get it out of my head especially when the gang came upon monologuing villains or argued with each other or even not using horses (cause it's racist don't you know?) made me think Python and I really think there should have been coconuts, the lack of coconuts was disappointing. <br><br><b>“My name is—”<br>“Don’t care,” I said.<br>He glared at me. “Don’t be rude.”<br>I sighed. “Sorry. Go ahead.”<br>“My name is Wan the Dark Hunter,” he said, squaring his shoulders.<br>I waited.<br>He looked at me, clearly expecting a reaction.<br>I waited some more.<br>“So,” he said, “that name should have inspired fear in you. You don’t look very fearful.”<br>I shrugged. “I don’t know who you are.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437641841ra/15606455.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also very disappointing that no villains got their limbs cut off. <br><br>Sam, Gary and Tiggy are my new favourite everything. Their adventures are adventures I really, really want to go on but I'm way happy to just be a causal observer. For reasons. But really all the characters make this the over the top joy that it was. The only one that I wanted to be killed with a ball of hell fire was Justin and he served a purpose. A ridiculously UST purpose. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437641774ra/15606441.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you have read any TJ Klune before you will recognise some similarities between the cast of this and previous book characters, but because of this setting, we get to see characters with absolutely no leashes and therefore they get to be totally outrageous. Outrageous like Gary the gay hornless unicorn. I can't even with Gary. I loved everything that came out of his mouth, even when he and Kevin were being utterly inapropro and scarred my brain he was still full of awesome. <br><br><b>“Oh calm the fuck down, Griselda,” Gary snapped. “We’re the only ones here, you ancient she-beast. You need to check yourself before you wreck yourself.”</b><br><br>^^^<br>Quotes like that made me lose my shit laughing. Gary is highly quotable and I have an urge to drop random quotes of his into real life conversations. That is one such quote. Replacing the name obviously! I have <i>literally</i> highlighted most of this book. It is <i>literally</i> the most highlighted book I've ever owned. <br><br>So The Lightning-Struck Heart is funny as all get out but as is TJ's way, there were ninja feelz and these ninja feelz felt more ninja than usual. This is many things, it's mainly comedy yes, it's comedy romance and a frustrating comedy romance at that. But it's also about loyalty and friendship and family and a lot of the time, the moments where Sam is hurt it was friends and family who brought the feelz and it was really very beautiful. <br><br><b>“There’s someone out there for you,” he said. “Someone who will love your hair and your words and your eyes and the way you still scrunch up your nose when you’re thinking hard on something. He will love you for all of the things that you are and all of the things you aren’t. He’ll love you beyond all reason and will be convinced that you hung the sun and moon. He will see the stars and wish for only you. Someone will love every single part of who you are, and my gods, I can’t wait for the day to meet him to tell him thank you.”</b><br><br>But mainly this has made me think about the logistics of a dragon and a unicorn doing the nasty. It's pretty much all the nookie we get until like the last 5% so it stays with you. I really need to stop thinking about it. Like I need to stop bad. Stupid Kevin. Stupid Gary. <br><br>I can't wait for more from this world and it has, for sure, been set up for more but to tide me over I need a TMIR reread and a Monty Python and The Holy Grail rewatch. <br><br><b>“Spaghetti face!” Tiggy cried. “Wizard Spaghetti Face.”<br>“He capitalized it,” Gary said. “Now it’s forever.”<br>“That’s a stupid fucking rule,” I grumbled.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437641883ra/15606487.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10876569375055280739" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText3161822225715026336" style="display:none"><b>BESTBOOKEVAH!!<br><br>5 HaveHeart4Evah Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442481576ra/16241804.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A absolute winner for me! EVERYONE.<br><br>Thanks to my friend Isabel for the rec because she is Awesome like that, and to T.J. Klune who is an Absolutely Extreme Talented Writer! <br><br>YEAH! <span id="freeTextContainer8207385718579119828">5 HUGE stars<br/><br/>Loved loved loved this one SO much!!! I just couldn't stop!! I've read it at work pretending I was working. I've read it on my way home from work. It was unpundownable! <br/><br/>This is the funniest book ever!!! I have laughed SO hard ALL the time while reading it!! It was the best banter I've ever had the pleasure to read. I mean, I couldn't stop the laughter even if I tried. SAM was the funniest character, but also the cornless unicorn and the half giant made this story unforgettable!!! And</span>
  <span id="freeText8207385718579119828" style="display:none">5 HUGE stars<br /><br />Loved loved loved this one SO much!!! I just couldn't stop!! I've read it at work pretending I was working. I've read it on my way home from work. It was unpundownable! <br /><br />This is the funniest book ever!!! I have laughed SO hard ALL the time while reading it!! It was the best banter I've ever had the pleasure to read. I mean, I couldn't stop the laughter even if I tried. SAM was the funniest character, but also the cornless unicorn and the half giant made this story unforgettable!!! And Ryan *sigh* Ryan was sweet and amazing!!! We get only a few hot scenes but I swear I am more than OK with this. I can't believe it. But we get SO many emotional moments and there were also some sad scenes. I expected my heart will get broken for Sam, only to explode with happiness the next moment. Amazing ending!!!<br /><br />This is without question the best book I've read this year and I am amazed by the writing! I already loved this author but I had NO idea he's that good. I adore his Wolfsong and Ravensong books. I adored all his books so far, but here we get so much delicious banter and crazy dialogues. Crazy, I am telling you!!!<br /><br />I've highlighted so much and only rereading some of them makes me snore with laughter. It was that good!!!<br /><br />Looking forward to reading the next books!!!</span>
