<div id="review_1799271384" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1799271384" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1799271384?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/28177280-the-lightning-struck-heart">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=funny-crack-up">funny-crack-up</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=m-m-and-m-f-m-and-m-m-f">m-m-and-m-f-m-and-m-m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=top-audios">top-audios</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=para-fantasy-series">para-fantasy-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=best-of-the-bestest">best-of-the-bestest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=favourites-2016">favourites-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=best-of-2016">best-of-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1799271384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18255364614415160900"><b>Big call...but I will say this is my favourite audio for 2016</b><br/><br/>When a brilliant author teams up with a brilliant narrator, <i>The Lightning-Struck Heart</i> is what you get. It was brilliantly, awesomely, fantastically magical. I loved the characters, storyline and setting for the story. It was easy to follow and the only times I had to rewind were when I missed a bit from laughing so hard.<br/><br/>I'll be honest (and hopefully not offend), this was the campest story I have ever read/listened to. The humour is ru</span>
  <span id="freeText18255364614415160900" style="display:none"><b>Big call...but I will say this is my favourite audio for 2016</b><br><br>When a brilliant author teams up with a brilliant narrator, <i>The Lightning-Struck Heart</i> is what you get. It was brilliantly, awesomely, fantastically magical. I loved the characters, storyline and setting for the story. It was easy to follow and the only times I had to rewind were when I missed a bit from laughing so hard.<br><br>I'll be honest (and hopefully not offend), this was the campest story I have ever read/listened to. The humour is rude, crude and socially unacceptable...I LOVED IT! <br><br>So, the story is about Sam the apprentice wizard his best mates Garry the hornless unicorn and Tiggy, the half-giant. Sam is set to be the King's wizard but is still in training. The group spend a lot of time being kidnapped and having to escape from the clutches of men who fall in love with Sam.<br><br>Poor Sam, if only he could be kidnapped by his one true love Ryan...but alas Ryan the King's Knight, is betrothed to the yucky Prince Justin.<br><br><i>The Lightning-Struck Heart</i> is a fantasy romance about two men who want and need each other but have every obstacle in their way. The journey towards their happiness is filled with humour but also a little heartache. <br><br>We are introduced to some very interesting characters, especially the dragon (with a deep Scottish accent that I loved), Morgan of Shadows, the Dark Lords and Big Momma - the drag queen brothel owner.<br><br>T.J. Klune writes a brilliant story and Michael Lesley is one of the most entertaining narrators I have ever heard. His ability to change his voice, act like a horse...I mean unicorn and <b>be</b> the characters was awe inspiring.<br><br>I loved <i>The Lightning-Struck Heart</i>. I don't read a lot of m/m and I know it is not for everyone, but there is only one intimate scene right at the end. If you don't mind campy humour this is definitely worth a try and I suggest you give the sample a go.<br><br>T.J. Klune...I'm a fan. Onwards...<br><br>***Sorry, this review is a bit dodgy. I'm on holidays at the beach and my motivation is pretty low to non-existent but I HAD to tell you about this story.***<br><br>To buy The Lightning-Struck Heart from Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2h94EKt">http://amzn.to/2h94EKt</a><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475811106i/20768637._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>I’m an Aussie chick who loves to read and review romance, drink coffee, be a <i>Style Setter</i> and stalk David Gandy. To see more of my reviews, fashion, food and pervathons -</b><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480249004i/21289598._SX540_.jpg" width="570" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2386908968" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9154384991386182675"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526068456i/25525069.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book... why did no one tell me about this book? I thought you guys were my friends! I thought you knew me! You had to know that it would be like magical rainbows made of the best chocolate ever to me. You all let me down.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526068456i/25525071._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, well for those of you who DIDN'T know about this book - you know - my GOOD friends - you need to read it. It is the funniest, craziest, sassiest, most original story ever! I'm not over-selling this at all.<br/><br/>I knew from the first line in this book that I was going to be </span>
  <span id="freeText9154384991386182675" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526068456i/25525069.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book... why did no one tell me about this book? I thought you guys were my friends! I thought you knew me! You had to know that it would be like magical rainbows made of the best chocolate ever to me. You all let me down.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526068456i/25525071._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, well for those of you who DIDN'T know about this book - you know - my GOOD friends - you need to read it. It is the funniest, craziest, sassiest, most original story ever! I'm not over-selling this at all.<br><br>I knew from the first line in this book that I was going to be enchanted:<br><br><b>
  <i>CHAPTER 1 <br>The Villain Monologues <br>“AND NOW, I will tell you of my plans to take over the Kingdom,” the evil wizard and total douchebag Lartin the Dark Leaf said with a cackle.</i>
</b><br><br>Yeah, love at first sight for me and this baby.<br><br>Our hero is Sam, a wizard's apprentice. His best friend is Gary, a gay hornless unicorn. Don't even think of calling him a horse. He gets pretty angry about that, and you don't want to see Gary angry.<br><br><b>
  <i>“He’s lucky I don’t have my horn back yet,” Gary muttered. “There’d be so much goring, it’d be unreal. It’d be like Gore City up in here."</i>
</b><br><br>Their third faithful companion is a half-giant who likes to smash. Consider him like Hulk. To start the story, Hulk smashes an annoying bad guy who monologues for way too long. This smashing will come back to haunt our friends over and over again as they adventure through magical forests and stuff. <br><br>Their quest: Saving the jerk-ass prince in time for his gay wedding to Ryan, the knight. Ryan is not just any knight, he's Sam's crush, so this wedding thing kind of sucks for him. To help Sam, the king sets up a party where he invites a bunch of gay bachelors to meet Sam in hopes of hooking him up. That's what you call a cool king. The king is awesome in so many ways. Here is where Sam is painting the king's portrait:<br><br><b>
  <i>King regally posed next to a stained-glass window. I had the easel set up a few feet away from him as I studied him closely, wanting to make sure I got his likeness just right. <br>“Oops,” I said.<br>“Oops,” the King said. “What oops?” <br>“Okay, so, how would you feel if you looked like you had boobs?”<br>“Am I busty?” <br>“Very. You also have three of them.” <br>“Good. Proceed.”<br>..."Oops"<br>"Oops?"<br>“So, hypothetically. Okay, that was a lie. It’s not hypothetical. I painted you to be as big as the Great White and you’re destroying Meridian City like a giant monster. My muse is obviously a surrealist and I must follow her into the artistic abyss.” <br>“Am I breathing fire?” <br>My eyes widened. “You could be. I have so much puce.” <br>“Make it so.”</i>
</b><br><br>Lol! Now I get why Gary and Sam call him a KILF. <br>He's a total KILF. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526068456i/25525070.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>As opposed to this king, the KIRFS <br>(King I'd Run From Screaming).<br>It's been years and yet still... seriously, Burger King, WTF?<br><br>Sam meets one guy that he likes a bit, Todd, so he goes to dinner with him. Unfortunately, there is not one thing in the restaurant that Sam can eat because it's Duck and Blueberry night and he's allergic to both. He doesn't hold that against Todd.<br><br><b>
  <i>“So. Todd.” <br>He nodded, throat working. <br>“How is your… life?” Smooth, that. And all encompassing.<br></i>
</b>(Did I mention Todd's a nervous wreck too? This date wins for most awkward of all times, but Sam wants to reassure Todd)<br><b>
  <i> “You’re off to a good start. Mostly. Maybe not the Food of Death thing.” </i>
</b><br>Better. That's some good encouragement.<br><br>Okay, so quick story:<br>We used to go to this one restaurant a lot and to get there, my husband would always take this shortcut through an alley and I would get all weird about it because it was (in my mind) sketchy. We nicknamed the alley "the alley of death" and the kids still tease me about it today. Mostly because I was nervous about a perfectly safe passageway in an affluent area that was well-lit and short. But, hey, in my defense, there could have been ax-carrying killers there, behind the Bed, Bath, and Beyond. I swear, my family are a bunch of assholes. Anyway, we use the "___of death" expression at my house a lot. I know you wanted to have this information.<br><br>But anyway. If there is still someone reading my rambling thoughts at this point...<br>The majority of the book is about the journey that Sam, Gary, Ryan, and the giant take. They meet up with a bunch of hilarious side-characters including a dragon named Kevin. And, sassiness is on every page. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I like your eyebrows,” I told him. “Way to buck societal norms of how eyebrows should normally look. Down with the system and all that.”</i>
</b><br><br>So.Much.Sass.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526068456i/25525072._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, to wrap this thing up, let me just say that if you are into sassy-gay-buddy-adventuring-fantasy-romance novels, this is the one for you. Oh, and there is some explicit gay sex involved, so either beware or be excited - it's up to you.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9154384991386182675" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1462348580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18131069424365313283">Re-Read Audible version 2.23.17: Even better the 2nd time around *as unbelievable as that may be* and that is without a doubt due to the brilliant audible performance of Michael Lesley! The huge array of characters and absolutely distinct personalities he had to give voice to was staggering and he delivered genuine perfection. I can't stress enough how stunning it was to hear these so-loved characters given life through their own voice, each one so completely what I imagined them as. Except for </span>
  <span id="freeText18131069424365313283" style="display:none">Re-Read Audible version 2.23.17: Even better the 2nd time around *as unbelievable as that may be* and that is without a doubt due to the brilliant audible performance of Michael Lesley! The huge array of characters and absolutely distinct personalities he had to give voice to was staggering and he delivered genuine perfection. I can't stress enough how stunning it was to hear these so-loved characters given life through their own voice, each one so completely what I imagined them as. Except for the ones that were unimaginable. *looking at you Dimitri* As stunning as it truly was, it was of course screamingly hilarious as only Verania and all its inhabitants can be. The only thing that was different for me here was how much more emotional the last part of the book was than I remembered, getting to hear everything in Sam's voice. I definitely got teary-eyed more this time around. But for all that, most of the tears were from laughter and I'll never be tired of this world. <br /><br />If you love this story, or even if you've never read it before, please treat yourself to the audiobook. It's not to be missed! Kisses to Josy for talking me into it! xxx <br /><br />*Original review*<br /><br />This was the most batshit thing I have ever read. It was like T.J. Klune won a bet to write the most over the top, outrageous and ridiculous thing he could possibly come up with. And he won <i>
  <b>BIG</b>
</i>, baby. It was The Most Awesome Thing Ever *and it's capitalized so it's official* *I swear I've laughed so much I've lost it*.<br /><br />Let me be clear. I am not in the least fond of over the top humor. For example, I'm the only person I know who doesn't like Will Ferrell. Not a fan, at all. But every damn thing about this got me. Sam the wizard apprentice and his best friends, Gary the hornless gay unicorn and Tiggy the half-giant, the gay fairy King, Kevin the sexually aggressive *and perverted* dragon, the fan club meetings in disguise *don't ask* and of course Knight Delicious Face. And that's not even close to everything that was so awesome. *sigh* This is excepting my sore abs, because throughout the whole book, I laughed so hard, the kind where your whole body shakes and you don't even make a noise, while tears run down your face and IT WAS GLORIOUS! *also except for the times I couldn't draw breath*<br /><br />I loved this so hard, my first T.J. Klune book and I'm an instant fangirl.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18131069424365313283" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4668918774152687524">My gods, he does it again. <br/>By now TJ Klune is among my absolute favorite authors, the man can write a dialogue, he can write a love story, and he can make you feel for the characters like no one else. Also his style is so distinct, that you have no doubt it is one of his books you are reading. If you are a fan of Bear, Otter and the Kid-series you will love this as well. Just be aware that some of the characters in this book is a tad bit more inappropriate (in the best possible way) compared to </span>
  <span id="freeText4668918774152687524" style="display:none">My gods, he does it again. <br />By now TJ Klune is among my absolute favorite authors, the man can write a dialogue, he can write a love story, and he can make you feel for the characters like no one else. Also his style is so distinct, that you have no doubt it is one of his books you are reading. If you are a fan of Bear, Otter and the Kid-series you will love this as well. Just be aware that some of the characters in this book is a tad bit more inappropriate (in the best possible way) compared to the other works of Mr. Klune. <br />I am absolutely positive that this is a book I will read again and again. I have not laughed as much as I did, reading a new book as I did reading TLSH.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2170019559" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3309264864976417662">I can understand why some people loved this book.<br/><br/>I can understand why some people found this book unreadable.<br/><br/>Klune is a clever and maybe even brilliant writer, and this book had some clever and brilliant moments. And some genuinely funny moments as well. But in general, his sense of humor is incompatible with mine. Most of the non-stop barrage of banter and joking was so crude and crass and gross and cringe-inducing, I'm probably lucky my face didn't freeze into an expression of horrified distas</span>
  <span id="freeText3309264864976417662" style="display:none">I can understand why some people loved this book.<br /><br />I can understand why some people found this book unreadable.<br /><br />Klune is a clever and maybe even brilliant writer, and this book had some clever and brilliant moments. And some genuinely funny moments as well. But in general, his sense of humor is incompatible with mine. Most of the non-stop barrage of banter and joking was so crude and crass and gross and cringe-inducing, I'm probably lucky my face didn't freeze into an expression of horrified distaste.<br /><br />I already own the second book. But the prospect of reading it seems exhausting. Unless someone promises me that the unicorn dies at the very beginning, I don't see myself picking it up.<br /><br />😖 &lt;-- My grossed-out expression got quite a workout while I was reading this.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1340112618" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15605734156756827403">This book is absolutely perfect! I've cried and cried... cried laughing, cried with sadness and I cried with happiness!<br/><br/>There is nothing in this book that I didn't love, there wasn't a single moment that I wanted to skip some pages, and there is this joy for reading such a fantastic story, fabulously written that captivated me from the beginning and that made me read it almost without pause.<br/><br/>All characters are amazing, even the Darks! All so peculiar and sensational! I love the MC's, Sam and Ryan </span>
  <span id="freeText15605734156756827403" style="display:none">This book is absolutely perfect! I've cried and cried... cried laughing, cried with sadness and I cried with happiness!<br><br>There is nothing in this book that I didn't love, there wasn't a single moment that I wanted to skip some pages, and there is this joy for reading such a fantastic story, fabulously written that captivated me from the beginning and that made me read it almost without pause.<br><br>All characters are amazing, even the Darks! All so peculiar and sensational! I love the MC's, Sam and Ryan are beautiful, but I must say that I adore Gary and Kevin!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440238460i/15950760._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will re-read it soon, I want to feel everything again!<br><br>Here it is something really awesome: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tjklunebooks.blogspot.pt/2015/09/tales-from-verania-tragic-life-of-lady.html?zx=6b7e925a1541986">http://tjklunebooks.blogspot.pt/2015/...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14794387597003980548"><i>Review written February 21, 2016</i><br/><br/><b>4 1/2 Stars - Indescribable and Incomparable. </a><br/><br/><i>The Lightning - Struck Heart</i>, a (M/M) book many friends talked about. A 400 pages novel published last summer (2015) by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune' title='T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>T.J. I'm impressed.<br/><br/>I listened to the 19:48 hrs audiobook nar</span>
  <span id="freeText14794387597003980548" style="display:none"><i>Review written February 21, 2016</i><br><br><b>4 1/2 Stars - Indescribable and Incomparable. Simply crazy Fun and Fabulous.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts%20gifs/image_zps9ozgadoc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455973908ra/18174319.gif" alt=" photo image_zps9ozgadoc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts%20gifs/image_zps9ozgadoc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455973908ra/18174319.gif" alt=" photo image_zps9ozgadoc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts%20gifs/image_zps9ozgadoc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455973908ra/18174319.gif" alt=" photo image_zps9ozgadoc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts%20gifs/image_zps9ozgadoc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455973908ra/18174319.gif" alt=" photo image_zps9ozgadoc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Lightning - Struck Heart</i>, a (M/M) book many friends talked about. A 400 pages novel published last summer (2015) by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a>, whose touching and hilarious funny M/M romances I already knew I liked. (Add an impressing average GR rating of 4.58 stars.) A "must read" in other words. — Yes ... they were all rigth. I'm impressed.<br><br>I listened to the 19:48 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6971140.Michael_Lesley" title="Michael Lesley" rel="nofollow noopener">Michael Lesley</a> and I'm totally exhausted but glad I did it. Kind of a EPIC "read"...<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>First I need to say that this is an incomparable story</b> and a wildly fun adventure book. A book about love, friendship and life's important questions and matters. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image_zps4myiafb1.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449953524i/17361303.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps4myiafb1.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>« Once upon a time, in an alleyway in the slums of the <i>City of Lockes</i>, a young and somewhat lonely boy named Sam Haversford turns a group of teenage douchebags into stone completely by accident. »</blockquote><br>Very short (I'll not even try to explain much more) is this novel about the young sorcerer-apprentice <b>Sam 'Wilds'</b> (former Haversford) in <i>Verania</i>. Sam who has a tremendous ability to get into all kinds of struggle, clutter and mess, despite the fact that everyone loves him, in this fantasy world. <br><br>Here are also all Sam's hilarious special friends. Sam's two besties; the witty quite flamboyant gay (without a horn) <b>Unicorn Gary</b> and the big-hearted (but slightly stupid) <b>Half-giant Tiggy</b>. In the center of this story is of course also Sam's secret big crush, the gorgeous <b>Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart</b> and unfortunately also <b>Prince Justin</b>, Ryan's betrothed. Halfway in to this story is a new friend, the horny and naughty (but enormous romantic) <b>Dragon Kevin</b>, taking a natural place in this lovely gang. <br><br>Those six aren't enough there are a big bunch of more wonderfully created second characters <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ — like Sam's mom &amp; dad, the old wise <i>Wizard Morgan</i>, the even older mighty <i>Wizard Kendall</i>, the very nice <i>King of Verania</i>, a transvestite shady brothel madam, some nasty fairy dark creatures as <i>The Darks</i> (which loves long monologues), some cute funny creatures (like tiny <i>Fairy Dimitri</i>), corn-eaters, and so on. — Loved them all, haha!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts/image_zpsqafnsf9j.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453278421ra/17805111.gif" alt=" photo image_zpsqafnsf9j.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br>*********************************************<br><br><b><i>The Lightning - Struck Heart</i> is a loooong story</b> <br>(almost 20 hours of listening). —Puff &amp; Huff!— It is basically a <u>fairytale comedy fantasy</u> and in many ways that sort of adventurous crazy story that even any younger teen fantasy/fairytale admirers would giggle and like about if there weren't for those (explicit) sex-jokes. There is of course (..it is after all written by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a>!!) a consistently adult gay romance theme in the bottom main topic. Not much heat workshop, more occasional shimmering sweet kisses, but after all there are a lot of hints and fantasies. <br><br><b>If anything is this a very talkative story</b>. (Imagine theater..) The charm is actually ultimately all this talking, talking, talking. There are joking, funny bantering, wacky discussions and long conversations that never ends — they all like to chatter and are sometimes quite near the limit of long-winded. Haha! I chuckled, giggled and felt the sweet fairytale atmosphere. Wow!!<br><blockquote>‘I turned slowly to Tiggy and Gary, my heart thundering in my chest. They were grinning at me, wide and toothy. “You… didn’t.” <br>“Oh, Sam,” Gary said. “You should never underestimate a unicorn and a giant.”</blockquote><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>The audiobook edition and the narrator..</b><br>The audiobook narrator <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6971140.Michael_Lesley" title="Michael Lesley" rel="nofollow noopener">Michael Lesley</a> is simply great (a perfect choice) and I guess he did this even funnier because this IS a fantastic funny read (or listening) for us adults, still young at heart and with the imagination there, to laugh with and truly enjoy. <br><br>My only complaint is that there are way to much of "Gary said..", "Tiggy said..", "X said.." and that bothered partly my listening. (About that topic: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I wish, when doing this audiobook, they had just skipped a lot of those unnecessary and often meaningless small "someone said" words. I felt this narrator so well created his very clear unique voices for each character and I'm sure I had understand 99% anyway without all those irritating mentions of who said what.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> )<br><blockquote>‘My dad growled, “If you touch my son, I'll cut off your arms and beat you with them.” <br>“Wow,” I said in complete adoration. “That was graphic and amazing.” <br>My mom said, “And I'll cut off your legs and shove them so far up your anus that you'll taste your feet at the back of your tongue.” <br>“Dudes,” I whispered to everyone. “That's my mom.” <br>Morgan said, “And I'll make your nipples explode.”<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image_zps4myiafb1.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449953524i/17361303.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps4myiafb1.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>Besides that mentioned little weak part is <i>The Lightning - Struck Heart</i> (obviously) a wonderful and fabulous well done audiobook. Applauses for Mr. Lesley. (I guess he had a hilarious time.)<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>I'll admit that I was restless at times</b> and I needed a couple of weeks to do those twenty audiobook hours. For me was this perfect as a daily one or two hours episode book. Sometimes there are too 'much' jokes, to much talking and it becomes a bit lengthy. So very crazy at times and I felt dizzy... But all in all, this is a hilarious funny and a well done story. Read (or listen) and enjoy. I guarantee laughter and giggles. RECOMMENDED!! <br><br>I will never forget all incomparably charming characters here. ~ I love you; Sam, Gary, Tiggy... There isn't enough time or place to mention all of you so just like in a (well prepared) acceptance speech: <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts%20gifs/image_zps9ozgadoc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455973908ra/18174319.gif" alt=" photo image_zps9ozgadoc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i>
  <b>No one mentioned no one forgotten, THANKS!</b>
</i><br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>I LIKE - indescribable, incomparable, but so much fun.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1207715970" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1207715970" />
    <a title="Ann" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21138490-ann"><img alt="Ann" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519708324p2/21138490.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1207715970?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ann" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ann" href="/user/show/21138490-ann">Ann</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/28485201-the-lightning-struck-heart">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=completely-fun">completely-fun</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=mm-rereads">mm-rereads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=fantasy-and-fairytales">fantasy-and-fairytales</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=all-time-favorite-mm">all-time-favorite-mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=boymeetsboy-review-books">boymeetsboy-review-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=completely-charming">completely-charming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21138490-ann?shelf=audible">audible</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1207715970" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14426520903682477990">ALL of the STARS. Every fucking one of them.<br/><br/>I spend a lot of time in my car commuting. I hate it. I like my job, I love the people I work with, but again, my commute? I hate it sooooo hard. So, when the commute from hell started a few years ago I got started listening to audio books. What better way is there to sit in traffic than to listen to a man tell me a story and at some point or 10 talk dirty to me? There is no better way, just so you know. When the request came through for a review on Th</span>
  <span id="freeText14426520903682477990" style="display:none">ALL of the STARS. Every fucking one of them.<br><br>I spend a lot of time in my car commuting. I hate it. I like my job, I love the people I work with, but again, my commute? I hate it sooooo hard. So, when the commute from hell started a few years ago I got started listening to audio books. What better way is there to sit in traffic than to listen to a man tell me a story and at some point or 10 talk dirty to me? There is no better way, just so you know. When the request came through for a review on The Lightning-Struck Heart I was ALL over that shit. I loved Michael Lesley’s narration of TJ’s Tell Me it’s Real so I was pretty happy. Then I started listening and I had so much fucking fun I was ecstatic!<br><br>If you’re a fan of TJ Klune when his manic humor is on high, then this book was written for you. Besides the absolute hilarity of his writing, he manages to sneak real feels in there giving the story and characters depth that sneak up on you like a tackle hug, make you happy in your heart and grin like a loon. This wasn’t just a story, it was an odyssey and it was ridiculously fun. I fell in love with every character, even the ones I should hate. I loved hating Tina at the fan club FFS.<br><br>As I said, I listened to the audiobook version and I do honestly believe that Michael Lesley IS the voice in TJ Klune’s head. I am truly amazed at how he managed to have a completely unique voice and tone for each character. You could take out every “he said”, “she said”, etc. and I would still have had no trouble distinguishing between who was talking at any given point. It was like being in the middle of a one man play that is so elaborate you forget you are only listening to one man. I laughed out loud so many times I’m going to have to listen to this one at least two more times to make sure I didn’t miss parts of the story for the LOL’s.<br><br>I was trying to figure out who my favorite character is and I gave up shortly into listening. Sam had me wrapped around his magical little finger and then Gary came along and I would follow his Unicornian buns anywhere. I was telling a friend about The Lightning-Struck Heart not long into listening. I walked into the office and he asked me what I was snortling about and I told him all about Sam and Ryan and Gary and Tiggy and etc. and etc. Now this friend is relatively new to the wonder that is the MM romance world. I’ve bought him some of my favorite books and steered him in the direction of authors I think he would like and he’s so damn happy about it all. He had no idea these stories and this world even existed. For me it’s amazing to have someone in my RL to talk books with on a daily basis!<br><br>Anywho, I babble. SO, I was telling him about this one and said, “Please, you have to listen to Gary for a second.” It was a scene where he and Sam were having a debate/discussion about Sam being gay fairy married and he looked at me with wide and happy eyes. I immediately went online and bought him a copy. We’ve been texting back and forth constantly ever since. He just met Kevin, I can’t wait to see what he has to say about Kevin. This is one of those treasures I’m going to keep in a safe place forever. It’s officially my Go-To, Feel-Good, Fuck-All-Y’all-I-Gotta-Fantasy-World-That-Needs-Me-To-Love-It-Right-Now Epics. And yes, all of that is capitalized because it’s a thing.<br><br><a href="http://boymeetsboyreviews.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384707178i/6936447.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>** a copy of this audiobook was provided for an honest review **</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14426520903682477990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer12114692441874788484"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453374780i/17818041.jpg' width='130' height='30' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh. My. God.<br/>What in the ever-loving hell was that? This book is so silly and ridiculous, it isn't even funny. And that is a total lie, because it's absolutely hilarious. Non-stop slapstick, banter, bickering, sassing, puns and innuendos.<br/><br/>This book was...<br/><br/><b>... absurd ...</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"You're about to feel my wrath."<br/>"Gross."<br/>"Not like that! Stop making it weird."<br/>"I'm talking to a hornless unicorn named Gary. It's already pretty weird."<br/>"Point."</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>... offensive ...</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"He was important to the Darks, Sam. No official </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12114692441874788484" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453374780i/17818041.jpg" width="130" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh. My. God.<br>What in the ever-loving hell was that? This book is so silly and ridiculous, it isn't even funny. And that is a total lie, because it's absolutely hilarious. Non-stop slapstick, banter, bickering, sassing, puns and innuendos.<br><br>This book was...<br><br><b>... absurd ...</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You're about to feel my wrath."<br>"Gross."<br>"Not like that! Stop making it weird."<br>"I'm talking to a hornless unicorn named Gary. It's already pretty weird."<br>"Point."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>... offensive ...</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>"He was important to the Darks, Sam. No official ranking. I guess it's easiest to say that he was beloved, in his way. People had an affection for him, even if he was a bit out there."<br>That... sort of made sense. "You mean like that special uncle that everyone just loves but is still kind of creepy because his touches last just a bit too long but he's always really apologetic about it and then he brings you pie?"<br>Morgan sighed. "I don't even know why I bother anymore."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>... dirty ...</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Is that what you want, pretty?" the dragon asked. "I'm a dragon, and maybe, if you're lucky, I'll be dragon my balls across your face later."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>... oddly sweet ...</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I love you," he said, kissing me sweetly.<br>I couldn't stop the smile if I'd wanted to. "Because I'm awesome."<br>He rolled his eyes. "Yes, Sam. Because you're awesome."<br>"Good," I said. "I love you too, even if you are an asshole."<br>"Heart boner," Gary moaned. "Throbbing heart boner."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>And those characters...<br><blockquote>
  <i>I looked at them. A hornless gay unicorn built out of rainbows and bitchiness. A half-giant who wanted to smash everything. A dragon who winked and flicked his tongue at me. A prince who I wanted to protect but also punch in the face. A knight I had a heart boner for.<br>"We're doomed," I moaned again. "Doooomed."</i>
</blockquote><br>Granted, the love interest and the adversary weren't the most memorable ones. The rest of the rabble, however, all the more. I've taken a particularly big shine to Morgan, Sam's asexual, sarcastic mentor, and Tiggy, the protective-destructive, mentally slow half-giant. ♡<br><br>The downside of all this craziness: It was terribly exhausting, and I couldn't read more than a few chapters at a time. About halfway through, I started skimming most of the conversations because sometimes, they were just too much for me to take. <br><br>Bottom line: It took me quite a while to get through this, but in the end it was totally worth it. <br>Though you'll definitely have to be in the right mood in order to enjoy the madness that is this book.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1946997461" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1480576220273353534">They say laughter is an instant vacation, and my sweet gods did I have an amazing one thanks to TJ Klune.<br/><br/>People just get the audio it is the best narration Ever! Worth every penny. I am now a Michael Lesley girl I fell in love with his voice. <br/><br/>Sweet Molasses.This Was Awesomely Funny (yes i capitalized.) Think Friends, Will & Grace, all rolled into 19 hours 49 minutes of laughter.<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504030922ra/23720320.gif' width='340' height='210' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And now the award for the clueless MC goes to SAM.. yoo-hoo...<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504031399ra/23720356.gif' width='340' height='210' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I loved this book so much. This book is about the frie</span>
  <span id="freeText1480576220273353534" style="display:none">They say laughter is an instant vacation, and my sweet gods did I have an amazing one thanks to TJ Klune.<br><br>People just get the audio it is the best narration Ever! Worth every penny. I am now a Michael Lesley girl I fell in love with his voice. <br><br>Sweet Molasses.This Was Awesomely Funny (yes i capitalized.) Think Friends, Will &amp; Grace, all rolled into 19 hours 49 minutes of laughter.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504030922ra/23720320.gif" width="340" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now the award for the clueless MC goes to SAM.. yoo-hoo...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504031399ra/23720356.gif" width="340" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I loved this book so much. This book is about the friendship, Love, Loyalty and adventures of Sam the awesome wizard apprentice, Gary the sassy sidekick and Tiggy the gentle giant. Their journey is epic and so funny. <br><br>Oh Sam I loved him so much he was this clueless sweet boy with a heart gold, awesome and quick with a joke, very loyal to his friends and family.. oohh! and he is in love with a Knight named Ryan. (who is unavailable,.. bummer) and he has no filter.. Sam was an amazing MC not once was i bored with his story..<br><br> <i> “Did I tell you he knew my name?”<br> “Sixteen times.”<br> “Oh. He said it twice.”<br> “Holy fuck on a stick.”<br> “He is.” I sighed.<br> “You want to lick his balls,” Gary said, just to see me sputter and flush brightly.</i><br><br><br>I loved Ryan too though sometimes I just wanted to shake him and tell him to stand up for himself and Sam.<br><br> <i>“I’m going to do so many spells,” I said, because it seemed impossible for me to stop. “You <br> won’t even believe how many spells I can do. Flora Bora Slam, motherfucker.” <br> “I want you to Flora Bora Slam me,” Ryan said.</i><br><br>Gary the hornless gay unicorn was sassy and a very pleasant character .... I laughed so hard at what he said and Michael Lesley brought the character to life by giving Gary a fitting voice.. Like Sam he too has no filter and says things like:<br><br> <i>“Hey, Ryan?” Gary asked. “If you’re so concerned with Sam’s… virtue and importance to the<br> Kingdom, why don’t you volunteer to be the chaperone? As Knight Commander of the King’s<br> Guard, no one is more qualified than you to ensure the safety of his butthole.”</i><br>And<br><br> <i>“I remember when you were a prude. My little boy who got flustered even saying the word <br> sex is now talking about rimming. Kids. You grow up so fast. Pretty soon you’ll be getting<br> fisted and I won’t know where the time has gone.”</i><br><br>I want my own Gary<br><br>Tiggy, Sam's parents, the King and Morgan were amazing secondary characters. As for Justin I still have not decided how I feel about him. <br><br>There was also a very pervy dragon called Kevin..<br><br><i>"Is that what you want, pretty?" the dragon asked. "I'm a dragon, and maybe, if you're lucky, <br> I'll be dragon my balls across your face later."</i><br><br>As much as it was a funny book there were some heartfelt moments and at times my heart broke for Sam, he covers his pain with humor and sass but it was right there for those who were keen to see.<br><br><b>“Because you’ve built up this shell around yourself. This exterior made up of sass and wordplay. You wear your heart on your sleeve, but you’ve disguised it so that only those that are close to you can ever hope of seeing it. You show so much without actually showing anything at all.”- The king to Sam </b><br><br><b>I need someone that I can be strong for. But I need someone who can also be strong for me.”- Sam</b><br><br><b>I Loved</b><br><br><i>To Mervin:<br> Don’t worry.<br> I’m a Sam Girl too.<br> Our secret?<br> Ryan Foxheart</i><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504030922ra/23720321.gif" width="340" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Sam and Gary lusting after Ryan that scene was hilarious..<br><br><i>Now was Knight Commander Ryan Foxheart climbing slowly out of the river, water cascading down his body, dripping over miles and miles of muscle.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cB61Oxk2L5XtQd/n4UGJiR2W8QtzCIZqBd0F2tYdF+kKgyl/4TenERHFLQJy9+4JtqF59HoZ9Y42MO5yMXaPSQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11086407333754533116">TJ KLUNE is a Lambda Literary Award-winning author (Into This River I Drown) and an ex-claims examiner for an insurance company. His novels include The House in the Cerulean Sea and The Extraordinaries. Being queer himself, TJ believes it's important—now more than ever—to have accurate, positive, queer representation in stories.</span>
